  // Events:
  // Gantenerumab subcutaneous dosing schedule: Every 4 weeks (28 days) for 1.5 years, starting at dose_start_age
  // Age-based events: Events are triggered when current_age_hours >= target_age
  // 4 weeks = 28/365 years 
  // 1.5 years = ~19 doses (1.5 * 365 / 28 = 19.5)
   E1: at (current_age_hours >= (dose_start_age - starting_age) * 365*24): SubCut_absorption = SubCut_absorption + SC_DoseAmount // Dose 1 at dose_start_age + 2 hours
  
  

  // Unit definitions:
  unit hour = 3600 second;
  unit per_hour = 1 / 0.000277778 second;
  unit nanomole_per_hour = 1e-9 mole / 0.000277778 second;
  unit nanomole = 1e-9 mole;
  unit litre_per_hour = litre / 0.000277778 second;
  unit nanomole_per_litre = mole / litre;
  unit per_nanomole_per_hour = 1 / (mole * 0.000277778 second);
  unit time_unit = hour;
end
